The communication server is based upon a well-known CouchDB database system and can be integrated with existing database setups, such as SAP, and can be configured separately to include services and to manage user accounts. The internal communication framework of Vizario allows for connectivity to different server-side services, such as MQTT Brokers for live-data visualization and import into Desktop and Hololens devices.\r\n\r\nVizario is not designed to produce fancy marketing-style visualizations in the first place. It was built by a group of AR experts with a combined 50+ years experience in Augmented Reality technology, with more than 2 years constant feedback from workers on the shopfloor. Therefore Vizario is considered a tool, which respects the importance of clear and understandable concepts to convey information to its users, and alleviates to the most extent any shortcomings in current interaction paradigms (e.g. complex gestures, voice control) in industrial environments (e.g. instead of textual input using QR codes for application login).\r\n\r\nVizario has a clear roadmap for the future, consisting of an increase in its feature set, as the understanding of Augmented Reality in public increases.
